	#tgcEvents for the imposition of a new government
	country_event = {
		id = 96085
		title = "EVTNAME96085" #Democracy
		desc = "EVTDESC96085"
		news = yes
		news_title = "EVTNAME96085_NEWS_TITLE"
		news_desc_long = "EVTDESC96085_NEWS_LONG"
		news_desc_medium = "EVTDESC96085_NEWS_MEDIUM"
		news_desc_short = "EVTDESC96085_NEWS_SHORT"
		picture = "unite"

		is_triggered_only = yes

		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTA96085" #We welcome the new regime.
			government = democracy
			ruling_party_ideology = liberal
			political_reform = universal_weighted_voting
			political_reform = population_equal_weight
			political_reform = yes_meeting
			political_reform = free_press
			political_reform = non_socialist
			political_reform = gerrymandering
			political_reform = non_secret_ballots
			clr_country_flag = communist_gov
			clr_country_flag = absolute_monarchy_gov
			clr_country_flag = semi_constitutional_monarchy_gov
			clr_country_flag = constitutional_monarchy_gov
			set_country_flag = democracy_gov
			clr_country_flag = presidential_dictatorship_gov
			clr_country_flag = fascist_gov
			clr_country_flag = anarcho_liberal_gov

			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_sphere_leader_of = THIS
					NOT = { has_country_flag = friendly_democracy }
				}
				diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -100 }
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = friendly_democracy
					truce_with = THIS
				}
				relation = { who = THIS value = 400 }
				diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = 100 }
				create_alliance = THIS
				clr_country_flag = friendly_democracy
			}
			capital_scope = {
				any_pop = {
					limit = { literacy = 0.2 }
					ideology = { factor = 0.1 value = liberal }
					ideology = { factor = -0.5 value = communist }
				}
			}
			any_pop = {
				ideology = { factor = -0.1 value = communist }
			}
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					ideology = reactionary
					factor = 6
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					ideology = communist
					factor = 6
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					ideology = fascist
					factor = 6
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					ideology = liberal
					factor = -4
				}
			}

			any_country = {
				limit = {
					war_with = THIS
				}
				end_war = THIS
			}
		}
	}
	#tgccrimeaCommunist Government Coup Puppets - The coup attempt
	country_event = {
		id = 443030
		title = "EVTNAME443030"
		desc = "EVTDESC443030"
		picture = "storming_palace_communists"

		is_triggered_only = yes

		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTA443030"
			prestige_factor = -0.25
			government = proletarian_dictatorship
			ruling_party_ideology = communist
			political_reform = none_voting
			political_reform = party_appointed
			political_reform = no_meeting
			political_reform = state_press
			political_reform = state_controlled
			political_reform = underground_parties
			political_reform = no_slavery
			political_reform = debtors_prisons
			social_reform = good_minimum_wage
			social_reform = eight_hours
			social_reform = good_subsidies
			social_reform = good_pensions
			set_country_flag = communist_gov
			clr_country_flag = absolute_monarchy_gov
			clr_country_flag = semi_constitutional_monarchy_gov
			clr_country_flag = constitutional_monarchy_gov
			clr_country_flag = democracy_gov
			clr_country_flag = presidential_dictatorship_gov
			clr_country_flag = fascist_gov
			clr_country_flag = anarcho_liberal_gov
			clr_country_flag = theocratic_government
			create_alliance = FROM
			relation = { who = FROM value = 200 }
			FROM = { diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = 100 } }
			any_country = { limit = { NOT = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } relation = { who = THIS value = -100 } }
			any_greater_power = { limit = { NOT = { government = proletarian_dictatorship } } diplomatic_influence = { who = THIS value = -100 } }

			ai_chance = {
				factor = 30
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
						OR = {
							FROM = { has_recently_lost_war = yes }
							FROM = { NOT = { military_score = 100 } }
						}
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 0.1
						NOT = { in_sphere = FROM }
					}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.4
					upper_house = {
						ideology = communist
						value = 0.1
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.5
					upper_house = {
						ideology = communist
						value = 0.15
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.6
					upper_house = {
						ideology = communist
						value = 0.2
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.7
					upper_house = {
						ideology = communist
						value = 0.25
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.8
					upper_house = {
						ideology = communist
						value = 0.3
					}
				}
				modifier = {
					factor = 1.9
					upper_house = {
						ideology = communist
						value = 0.4
					}
				}
			}
		}

		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTB443030"
			add_country_modifier = { name = small_country_draft duration = 730 }
			end_military_access = FROM
			leave_alliance = FROM

			FROM = { country_event = { id = 443031 days = 2 } }

			add_country_modifier = { name = no_freedom duration = 2920 }

			capital_scope = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.1 value = communist } } }

			random_pop = { limit = { pop_majority_ideology = communist }
				random_list = {
					34 = { reduce_pop = 0.98 }
					33 = { reduce_pop = 0.97 }
					33 = { reduce_pop = 0.96 }
					}
				random_list = {
					34 = { ideology = { factor = 0.1 value = conservative } }
					33 = { ideology = { factor = 0.2 value = conservative } }
					33 = { ideology = { factor = 0.3 value = conservative } }
					}
				random_list = {
					34 = { ideology = { factor = -0.1 value = communist } }
					33 = { ideology = { factor = -0.15 value = communist } }
					33 = { ideology = { factor = -0.2 value = communist } }
					}
				}

			random_pop = { limit = { pop_majority_ideology = communist }
				random_list = {
					34 = { reduce_pop = 0.98 }
					33 = { reduce_pop = 0.97 }
					33 = { reduce_pop = 0.96 }
					}
				random_list = {
					34 = { ideology = { factor = 0.1 value = conservative } }
					33 = { ideology = { factor = 0.2 value = conservative } }
					33 = { ideology = { factor = 0.3 value = conservative } }
					}
				random_list = {
					34 = { ideology = { factor = -0.1 value = communist } }
					33 = { ideology = { factor = -0.15 value = communist } }
					33 = { ideology = { factor = -0.2 value = communist } }
					}
				}

			random_pop = { limit = { pop_majority_ideology = communist }

	# 880130 - Party Scandal - Reactionary
	country_event = {
		id = 880130
		title = "EVTNAME880130"
		desc = "EVTDESC880130"
		picture = "news"

		trigger = {
			civilized = yes
			NOT = {
				press_rights = state_press
				political_parties = underground_parties
				has_country_modifier = ruling_party_scandal
				has_country_modifier = party_scandal_evidence
			}
			OR = {
				reactionary = 10
				any_owned_province = { reactionary = 20 }
			}
		}

		mean_time_to_happen = {
			months = 400
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.75
				election = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
				NOT = { press_rights = free_press }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				election = yes
				ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { average_consciousness = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = { average_consciousness = 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				average_consciousness = 6
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				average_consciousness = 8
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				average_consciousness = 9
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				reactionary = 25
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				reactionary = 50
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				reactionary = 75
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				NOT = {	ruling_party_ideology = reactionary }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.7
				NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = reactionary }
				political_parties = harassment
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = reactionary }
				political_parties = gerrymandering
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = reactionary }
				political_parties = non_secret_ballots
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.9
				NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = reactionary }
				press_rights = censored_press
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
				political_parties = harassment
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
				political_parties = gerrymandering
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
				political_parties = non_secret_ballots
			}
		}

		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTA880130"
			random_owned = {
				limit = {
					owner = { ruling_party_ideology = reactionary }
				}
				owner = {
					prestige = -5
					plurality = -1
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = ruling_party_scandal
						duration = 730
					}
				}
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					location = { is_colonial = no }
					reactionary = 10
				}
				ideology = {
					value = reactionary
					factor = -0.1
				}
			}
			any_pop = {
				limit = {
					location = { is_colonial = no }
				}
				scaled_consciousness = {
					ideology = reactionary
					factor = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	campaigning_middle_class = {

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = poor } ideology = { factor = -0.02 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = poor } ideology = { factor = -0.02 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = poor } ideology = { factor = -0.02 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = poor } ideology = { factor = -0.02 value = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = poor } ideology = { factor = -0.02 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { strata = poor } ideology = { factor = -0.02 value = progressive } } } }

	campaigning_primary_culture = {
		picture = "campaigning_primary_culture"

		potential = {
			has_country_flag = show_campaigning_decision
			ai = no
			
			#Every gov type can do this

			OR = { citizenship_policy = residency citizenship_policy = limited_citizenship }
		}
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = party_campaigning_timer }
		}
		effect = {
		
			#Timer
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { election = no } }
				owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 182 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { election = yes } }
				owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 50 } }
			}
			
			#Majority races are pleased
			any_pop = {
				limit = { is_culture_group = THIS }
				militancy = -2
				consciousness = -2
			}
			
			#Minority races get angry
			any_pop = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } }
				militancy = 2
				consciousness = 2
			}
			
			#Progressive and liberals are not happy
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = liberal
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = progressive
				}
			}
			
			#Gain negative international attention
			any_country = {
				limit = { is_vassal = no citizenship_policy = full_citizenship }
				relation = { who = THIS value = -10 }
			}
			
			#Boost ideology support from culture group
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = traditionalist } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = liberal } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = communist_social } } } }
			
			#Reduce ideology support for non culture groups
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = traditionalist } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = socialist } } } }

			}
			
			#Reduce ideology support from culture group
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = liberal } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_culture_group = THIS } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = communist_social } } } }

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { is_culture_group = THIS } } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = traditionalist } } } }

		#cweCampaign for national religion
	campaigning_national_religion = {
		picture = "campaigning_national_religion"

		potential = {
			has_country_flag = show_campaigning_decision
			ai = no
			
			#Every gov type can do this
			
			#Country is not secular
			has_country_flag = desecularized
			
			#Religious party
			religious_policy = moralism
			
			#Religion is less of a politicised issue in highly educated nations
			NOT = { literacy = 0.20 }
		}
		allow = {
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = party_campaigning_timer }
		}
		effect = {
		
			#Timer
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { election = no } }
				owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 182 } }
			}
			random_owned = {
				limit = { owner = { election = yes } }
				owner = { add_country_modifier = { name = party_campaigning_timer duration = 50 } }
			}
			
			#State religion pops are happy
			any_pop = {
				limit = { is_state_religion = yes }
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -2
					issue = moralism
				}
				scaled_consciousness = {
					factor = -2
					issue = moralism
				}
			}
			
			#Non state religion pops are angry
			any_pop = {
				limit = { is_state_religion = no }
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					issue = secularized
				}
				scaled_consciousness = {
					factor = 2
					issue = secularized
				}
				
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					issue = pro_atheism
				}
				scaled_consciousness = {
					factor = 2
					issue = pro_atheism
				}
			}
			
			#Progressive and liberals are not happy
			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = liberal
				}
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = 2
					ideology = progressive
				}
			}
			
			#Gain negative international attention
			any_country = {
				limit = { is_vassal = no OR = { religious_policy = pro_atheism religious_policy = secularized } }
				relation = { who = THIS value = -10 }
			}
			
			#Boost ideology support from culture group
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = yes } ideology = { factor = 0.04 value = communist_social } } } }
			
			#Reduce ideology support for non culture groups
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = no } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = populist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = no } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = nationalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = no } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = traditionalist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = no } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = conservative } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = no } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = liberal } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = no } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = no } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = no } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = socialist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = no } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = communist } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { is_state_religion = no } ideology = { factor = -0.04 value = communist_social } } } }

	campaigning_secularism = {

			#Religion is less of a politicised issue in highly educated nations
			NOT = { literacy = 0.20 }
		}

			}

				limit = { is_state_religion = yes }
				scaled_militancy = {
					factor = -2
					issue = secularized
				}
				scaled_consciousness = {
					factor = -2
					issue = secularized
				}

					issue = pro_atheism
				}
				scaled_consciousness = {

					issue = pro_atheism
				}

				}

				}

					ideology = liberal

				}

			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.02 value = big_tent } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.02 value = progressive } } } }
			random_owned = { limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } owner = { any_pop = { limit = { has_pop_religion = secularism } ideology = { factor = 0.02 value = socialist } } } }

		}

		}

#cweAnger against Conscription
country_event = {
	id = 1512349
	title = "Controversy over Conscription"
	desc = EVTDESC1512349
	picture = "conscription_controversy"

	trigger = {

		OR = { 
			lgbt_rights = lgbt_promoted
			lgbt_rights = lgbt_allowed
			lgbt_rights = lgbt_equal_rights
		}

		war = no
		has_recently_lost_war = no

		average_militancy = 2

		OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy government = hms_government government = hms_government1 }

		OR = {
			pop_majority_ideology = liberal
			pop_majority_ideology = progressive
			has_country_modifier = massive_government_corruption
			has_country_modifier = large_government_corruption
			has_country_modifier = medium_government_corruption
		}

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 60 
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 average_militancy = 2 }
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 average_militancy = 3 }
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 average_militancy = 4 }
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 average_militancy = 5 }
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 average_militancy = 6 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Maintain our current conscription laws"

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.01 value = conservative } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.01 value = big_tent } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.01 value = socialist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.01 value = traditionalist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.01 value = populist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.01 value = nationalist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.01 value = progressive } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.01 value = liberal } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.01 value = communist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.01 value = communist_social } } }
		}
		
		#Increase militancy and consciousness
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = traditionalist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 2 ideology = traditionalist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = conservative } scaled_militancy = { factor = 2 ideology = conservative } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = liberal } scaled_militancy = { factor = 2 ideology = liberal } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = big_tent } scaled_militancy = { factor = 2 ideology = big_tent } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = progressive } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = progressive } scaled_militancy = { factor = 2 ideology = progressive } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = socialist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 2 ideology = socialist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = communist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 2 ideology = communist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = communist_social } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = communist_social } scaled_militancy = { factor = 2 ideology = communist_social } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = nationalist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 2 ideology = nationalist } } } }
		random_owned = { limit = { owner = { NOT = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } } } owner = { any_pop = { scaled_consciousness = { factor = 2 ideology = populist } scaled_militancy = { factor = 2 ideology = populist } } } }

		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0.9 
			modifier = { 
				factor = 0 
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal ruling_party_ideology = progressive } 
			} 
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = "Loosen our conscription laws"

		#Officers get angry
		any_pop = {
			limit = { type = officers }
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 10
				ideology = nationalist
			}
			scaled_militancy = {
				factor = 5
				ideology = populist
			}
		}

		#two_year_draft to one_year_draft
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { lgbt_rights = lgbt_equal_rights } }
			owner = { political_reform = gender_neutrallity }
		}

		#three_year_draft to two_year_draft
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { lgbt_rights = lgbt_allowed } }
			owner = { political_reform = lgbt_equal_rights }
		}

		#mandatory_service to three_year_draft
		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { lgbt_rights = lgbt_promoted } }
			owner = { political_reform = lgbt_allowed }
		}

		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }

	}

}
#cweAnger against Conscription
country_event = {
	id = 1512350
	title = "Calls to Abolish Conscription"
	desc = EVTDESC1512349
	picture = "conscription_controversy"

	trigger = {

		lgbt_rights = gender_neutrallity

		war = no
		has_recently_lost_war = no

		NOT = { any_owned_province = { has_province_modifier = unstable_region } }

		OR = { government = democracy government = democracy1 government = socialist_democracy government = hms_government government = hms_government1 }

		OR = {
			pop_majority_ideology = liberal
			pop_majority_ideology = progressive
			has_country_modifier = massive_government_corruption
			has_country_modifier = large_government_corruption
			has_country_modifier = medium_government_corruption
		}

	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 60 
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 average_militancy = 2 }
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 average_militancy = 3 }
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 average_militancy = 4 }
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 average_militancy = 5 }
		modifier = { factor = 0.75 average_militancy = 6 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Maintain our current conscription laws"

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.05 value = conservative } } }
		}

}

}

modifier = { factor = 4 OR = { has_country_modifier = low_government_corruption has_country_modifier = low_government_corruption } }

modifier = { factor = 3 has_country_modifier = nepohigh }

modifier = { factor = 0.5 election = yes }

#cweGovernment in Chaos
country_event = {
	id = 1610116
	title = "$COUNTRY_ADJ$ Government in Chaos"
	desc = EVTDESC1610116
	picture = "government_in_chaos"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
	
		#Minority government
		OR = {

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = traditionalist pop_majority_ideology = conservative } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist ruling_party_ideology = conservative } 
			} 

			AND = { 
				NOT = { pop_majority_ideology = big_tent }
				ruling_party_ideology = big_tent
			} 

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = socialist pop_majority_ideology = communist pop_majority_ideology = communist_social } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist ruling_party_ideology = communist ruling_party_ideology = communist_social }
			} 

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = liberal pop_majority_ideology = progressive } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = liberal ruling_party_ideology = progressive }
			}

			AND = { 
				NOT = { OR = { pop_majority_ideology = nationalist pop_majority_ideology = populist } }
				OR = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist ruling_party_ideology = populist }
			}
		
		}
		
		NOT = { publishing_rights = censored_publishing }
		
		average_militancy = 5
		average_consciousness = 4
		
		OR = {
			has_country_modifier = leadership_chaos
			
			#If there is a party scandal
			has_country_modifier = ruling_party_scandal
			has_country_modifier = party_scandal_evidence

	}

			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.03 value = conservative } } }
		}

			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.03 value = big_tent } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.03 value = socialist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.03 value = traditionalist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.03 value = populist } } }

country_event = {
	id = 82990032
	title = "Indonesian mass killings of 19651966"
	desc = EVTDESC1412245
	picture = "ido_killings"

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = IDO
		year = 1965
		NOT = { year = 1990 }
		
		war = no
		
		#Cold War
		has_global_flag = blocsenabled
		
		#Is not the USI
		government = democracy
		is_vassal = no
		
		#Sukarno's party
		ruling_party_ideology = nationalist
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = "Unleash the massacre!"
		prestige = -100
		badboy = 5
		
		#USA gains influence over Indonesia
		USA = { 
			diplomatic_influence = { who = IDO value = 50 } 
			relation = { who = IDO value = 100 }
		}
		
		any_pop = {
			ideology = {
				factor = -0.10
				value = communist
			}
		}

		#Dirty War
		add_country_modifier = { name = dirty_war duration = 730 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}

	option = {
		name = "Leave the communists alone"
		
		#Add more communist support!
		any_pop = { 
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.10
				value = communist
			}
		}
		
		#Add more socialist support!
		any_pop = { 
			ideology = {
				factor = 0.10
				value = socialist
			}
		}
		
		#USSR gains influence over Indonesia
		RUS = { 
			diplomatic_influence = { who = IDO value = 50 } 
			relation = { who = IDO value = 100 }
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}

}

	id = 17730
	title = "EVTNAME17730"
	desc = "EVTDESC17730"

		is_ideology_enabled = communist
		is_colonial = no
		owner = { NOT = {	OR = { pop_majority_religion = sunni pop_majority_religion = shiite } } }
		NOT = { controlled_by = REB }
		OR = {
			socialist = 20
			communist = 10
		}
		OR = {
			has_pop_type = artisans
			has_pop_type = clerks
			has_pop_type = craftsmen
			has_pop_type = labourers
		}

			average_militancy = 6
			has_province_modifier = militant_trade_union
			has_province_modifier = province_strike
			NOT = { poor_strata_life_needs = 0.7 }
		}

#cweFull blown epidemic in $COUNTRY$ - If all cored state_capitals have the virus
country_event = {
	id = 1412015
	title = "Full Blown Epidemic in $COUNTRY$"
	desc = EVTDESC1412015
	picture = "new_virus_spreads"

	trigger = {
	
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = { 
				has_province_modifier = virus_outbreak 
				has_province_modifier = virus_outbreak_deadly 
			}
		}
	
		NOT = {
			any_owned_province = {
				is_state_capital = yes
				is_core = THIS
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						has_province_modifier = virus_outbreak 
						has_province_modifier = virus_outbreak_deadly 
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		NOT = { has_country_flag = full_blown_epidemic }
		
	}

	option = {
		name = "This reflects badly on the government!"
		
		set_country_flag = full_blown_epidemic
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = local_epidemic duration = 1825 }
		
		prestige_factor = -0.01

		#Reduce government support

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = conservative } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.05 value = conservative } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.05 value = big_tent } } }
		}

		random_owned = {

			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.05 value = socialist } } }
		}

		random_owned = {

country_event = {
	id = 1412018
	title = "Virus Epidemic Response Criticised"
	desc = EVTDESC1412018
	picture = "new_virus_spreads3"

	trigger = {
	
		#Event not already fired
		NOT = { has_country_flag = virus_response_criticised }
	
		#Has virus controls
		has_country_flag = enable_virus_controls
	
		#Has virus in country
		any_owned_province = {
			OR = { 
				has_province_modifier = virus_outbreak 
				has_province_modifier = virus_outbreak_deadly 
			}
		}
		
		OR = {
			#Do not have strong virus controls
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = virusmedium
					has_country_modifier = virushigh
				}
			}
			
			#Full blown epidemic and minimal virus controls
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = virusno
				has_country_flag = full_blown_epidemic
			}
			
			#Did not inform WHO
			NOT = { has_country_flag = who_alerted_to_new_virus }
		}
		
		has_global_flag = epidemic_start
		
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 2
		modifier = { publishing_rights = firewall_publishing factor = 3 }
		modifier = { publishing_rights = censored_publishing factor = 6 }

country_event = {
	id = 1512206
	title = "Disastrous War"
	desc = EVTDESC1512206
	picture = "lost_war_party_hit"

	trigger = {

		war = no

		NOT = { has_country_flag = this_won_CB }
		has_country_flag = this_lost_CB

		has_country_flag = country_at_war

	}

	option = {
		name = "The people blame the government for the defeat!"
		clr_country_flag = country_at_war
		
		#Clear UN peace flag
		clr_country_flag = UN_demands_peace_flag
		clr_country_flag = country_that_UN_demands_peace_flag
		remove_country_modifier = called_allies_un
		remove_country_modifier = stop_un_spam
		remove_country_modifier = resolution_vetoed_unsc
		
		#Clear AI is more trigger happy with nukes flag
		clr_country_flag = more_willing_nuke_behaviour
		
		#Clear capitulation flag for the AI
		clr_country_flag = nation_has_capitulated

		#Clear Colonial Overlord markers
		clr_country_flag = colonial_overlord_at_war

		#Clear aggressor flag
		clr_country_flag = this_is_aggressor

		#Clear CB bypass flag
		clr_country_flag = bypass_normal_CB_requirements

		#Remove CB markers
		clr_country_flag = this_won_CB
		clr_country_flag = this_lost_CB

		#Remove strategic bombardment flag
		clr_country_flag = strategic_bombardment

		#Great Patriotic War gives post war war exhaustion

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { has_country_modifier = fanatic_army } }
			owner = { remove_country_modifier = fanatic_army war_exhaustion = 50 any_pop = { dominant_issue = { value = pacifism factor = 0.25 } } }
		}

		#Reset satellites
		clr_country_flag = destroy_satelllites

		remove_country_modifier = constricting_international_trade
		remove_country_modifier = constrict_international_trade_modifier

		}

		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = big_tent } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.25 value = big_tent } } }
		}

			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = socialist } }

		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = traditionalist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.25 value = traditionalist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = populist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.25 value = populist } } }
		}

		random_owned = { 
			limit = { owner = { ruling_party_ideology = nationalist } }
			owner = { any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.25 value = nationalist } } }
		}

		random_owned = {

country_event = {
	id = 1512280
	title = "Inconclusive War"
	desc = EVTDESC1512280
	picture = "draw_war_party_hit"

	trigger = {
		war = no
		has_country_flag = country_at_war
		
		#Country is an aggressor
		has_country_flag = this_is_aggressor
		
		#Country did not fulfil or accept any wargoals
		OR = { 
		
			AND = { has_country_flag = this_won_CB has_country_flag = this_lost_CB }
		
			AND = { 
				NOT = { has_country_flag = this_won_CB }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = this_lost_CB }
			}
		
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = "We will prevail eventually!"
		clr_country_flag = country_at_war
		
		#Clear UN peace flag
		clr_country_flag = UN_demands_peace_flag
		clr_country_flag = country_that_UN_demands_peace_flag
		remove_country_modifier = called_allies_un
		remove_country_modifier = stop_un_spam
		remove_country_modifier = resolution_vetoed_unsc

	#TGCDescription: Carlos Lopez coup
	country_event = {
		id = 700002
		title = "EVTNAME700002"
		desc = "EVTDESC700002"
		picture = "lopez_dictator"

		fire_only_once = yes

		trigger = {
			tag = PRG
			exists = yes
			year = 1844
			has_country_flag = carlos_lopez_elected
			NOT = { year = 1860 }
			NOT = { has_country_modifier = solano_lopez_industrialization }
		}

		mean_time_to_happen = { months = 2 }

		immediate = { clr_country_flag = carlos_lopez_elected }

		# Dictatorship
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTA700002"

			add_country_modifier = { name = solano_lopez_industrialization duration = 1825 }
			set_country_flag = carlos_lopez_dictator
			ruling_party_ideology = reactionary
			government = presidential_dictatorship
			## Reforms ##
				political_reform = party_appointed
				political_reform = none_voting
				political_reform = no_meeting
				political_reform = underground_parties
				political_reform = state_press
			## Election Flags ##
				clr_country_flag = tory_election_win
				clr_country_flag = socialist_election_win
				clr_country_flag = liberal_election_win
				clr_country_flag = communist_election_win
				clr_country_flag = fascist_election_win
				clr_country_flag = reactionary_election_win
				clr_country_flag = anarcho_liberal_election_win
			## Prime Ministers ##
				remove_country_modifier = expert_diplomat
				remove_country_modifier = successful_industrialist
				remove_country_modifier = ivory_tower_intellectual
				remove_country_modifier = man_of_the_people
				remove_country_modifier = landed_gentleman
				remove_country_modifier = military_man
				remove_country_modifier = lord_admiral
				remove_country_modifier = raving_loon
				remove_country_modifier = luddite
				remove_country_modifier = great_statesman
				remove_country_modifier = backroom_boy
				remove_country_modifier = great_reformer
				remove_country_modifier = gauche_buffoon
				remove_country_modifier = administrative_genius
				remove_country_modifier = visionary_thinker
				remove_country_modifier = competent_placeholder
				remove_country_modifier = imperious_autocrat
				remove_country_modifier = prince_of_terror
				remove_country_modifier = efficient_sociopath
				remove_country_modifier = pig_headed_isolationist
				remove_country_modifier = ambitious_union_boss
				remove_country_modifier = dour_economist
			any_pop = { ideology = { factor = -0.2 value = liberal } }

			any_neighbor_country = { relation = { who = THIS value = -50 } }

			ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		}

		# Democracy
		option = {
			name = "EVTOPTB700002"

			any_pop = {
				scaled_militancy = {
					ideology = conservative
					factor = 9
				}
				scaled_militancy = {

					factor = 9
				}
				ideology = {
					factor = 0.3
					value = liberal
				}
			}

			ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		}

				has_province_modifier = militant_trade_union

			}
		}
	}

		months = 300
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			poor_strata_everyday_needs = 1.0
		}

			factor  = 0.9

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_modifier = province_strike
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.7
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_modifier = militant_trade_union
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			average_militancy = 4
		}

			factor = 0.9
			socialist = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			socialist = 10
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			socialist = 15
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { social_reform_want = 0.05 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			social_reform_want = 0.05
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			social_reform_want = 0.1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			average_consciousness = 7
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			OR = {
				nationalvalue = nv_equality
				nationalvalue = nv_unity
				nationalvalue = nv_prosperity
				nationalvalue = nv_fraternity
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				nationalvalue = nv_liberty
				nationalvalue = nv_freedom
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			OR = {
				nationalvalue = nv_order
				nationalvalue = nv_productivity
				nationalvalue = nv_dominion
			}
			NOT = {
				ruling_party_ideology = socialist
				ruling_party_ideology = communist
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			economic_policy = laissez_faire
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			war = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = {
				average_consciousness = 3
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {

		plurality = -2

				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {

						has_province_modifier = worker_union
						has_province_modifier = province_strike
					}
				}
			}
			any_owned = {
				remove_province_modifier = labor_union
				remove_province_modifier = militant_trade_union
				remove_province_modifier = worker_union
				remove_province_modifier = strike_solution
				remove_province_modifier = province_strike
			}

					value = reactionary

				}

					ideology = socialist

			}
		}
	}

					has_province_modifier = labor_union
					has_province_modifier = militant_trade_union

				}
			}
			state_scope = {

					militancy = 2

				}

						value = socialist
						factor = 0.1
					}
					scaled_militancy = {
						ideology = socialist
						factor = -2
					}
				}

	    prestige = 25

		2100 = { add_core = XHO }
		2672 = { add_core = XHO }
		
		#SAF releases XHO territories
		SAF = {
			any_owned = {
				limit = { 
					OR = { 
						province_id = 2098 
						province_id = 2672 
					}
				}
				secede_province = XHO
			}
		}
	}

		war = no

		NOT = { government = proletarian_dictatorship1 }

		NOT = { has_country_flag = latin_debt_crisis }

		NOT = { has_country_modifier = financial_crisis }

		OR = { has_country_flag = south_american_isi has_country_flag = importfocus }

	}

	immediate = { remove_country_modifier = economic_boom }

	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		months = 60
		modifier = { 
			factor = 0.1 
			any_neighbor_country = { has_country_modifier = financial_crisis } 
		}
	}

			}

	}

		is_core = THIS

		NOT = {
			has_province_modifier = national_assimilation_acceptance
			has_province_modifier = nationalist_agitation
		}

		owned_by = THIS
		is_colonial = no
		owner = {
			civilized = yes
			war = no
			NOT = { citizenship_policy = full_citizenship }
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 180
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_primary_culture = no
			is_accepted_culture = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_primary_culture = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_accepted_culture = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = nationalist_agitation }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_province_modifier = national_assimilation_rejection
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = national_assimilation_rejection }
			any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = national_assimilation_rejection }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_neighbor_province = { has_province_modifier = national_assimilation_acceptance }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_militancy = 2
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_militancy = 3
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_militancy = 4
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			average_militancy = 5
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = EVT_2620_A
		remove_province_modifier = national_assimilation_rejection
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = national_assimilation_acceptance
			duration = -1
		}
		any_pop = {
			consciousness = -3
			militancy = -2
		}
		any_pop = {
			limit = {
				is_primary_culture = no
				is_accepted_culture = no
			}
			ideology = {
				value = nationalist
				factor = -0.25
			}
		}
	}
}

			ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
		}

#CWE #soviet_union - Brezhnevs Resignation.txt 
country_event = { # Resignation of Leonid Brezhnev?
	id = 9001475
	title = "Resignation of Leonid Brezhnev?"
	desc = EVT_9001475_DESC
	picture = "brezhnev_doctrine"
  
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		year = 1974
		NOT = { year = 1976 }
		
		government = proletarian_dictatorship
		is_vassal = no
		war = no
		
		has_country_flag = leonid_brezhnev
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 5 }

	option = {
		name = "Continue despite everything."
		
		poor_strata = { consciousness = 3 }
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.9 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Select Dinmukhamed Kunaev (Conservative-Moderate)."
		
		set_country_flag = dinmukhamed_kunaev
		clr_country_flag = leonid_brezhnev
		
		#Party elites are happy & rise of reformism
		any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist } militancy = -3 consciousness = -3 }
		any_pop = { limit = { strata = poor } ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist_social } militancy = 2 consciousness = 2 }
		
		#Reduction of nationalism
		any_pop = { limit = { NOT = { culture = russian } } ideology = { factor = -0.05 value = nationalist } consciousness = -5 militancy = -5 }
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.05 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Select Yuri Andropov (Reformist)."
		
		set_country_flag = yuri_andropov
		set_country_flag = brezhnev_resignation
		clr_country_flag = leonid_brezhnev
		clr_country_flag = yuri_andropov_3
		
		#Rise of reformism & instability from early reforms
		any_pop = { limit = { strata = rich } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = communist_social } militancy = 5 consciousness = 5 }
		any_pop = { limit = { strata = middle } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = progressive } }
		any_pop = { limit = { strata = poor } ideology = { factor = 0.10 value = socialist } }
		add_country_modifier = { name = military_strife duration = 3650 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = political_strife duration = 3650 }
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.05 }
	}
	
}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		year = 2041
		NOT = { year = 2043 }
		
		OR = {
			government = proletarian_dictatorship
			government = socialist_democracy
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { months = 6 }

	option = {
		name = "The sacrifice of the Soviet people."
		prestige = 300
		
		any_pop = { 
			consciousness = -2 
			militancy = -3
			ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist }
			ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = nationalist } 
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.6 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "Showing the horror of Fascism"
		prestige = 300
		
		any_pop = { 
			consciousness = -3 
			militancy = -3
			ideology = { factor = -0.05 value = nationalist }
			ideology = { factor = -0.05 value = populist } 
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.3 }
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "The inflexibility of Stalin."
		
		badboy = 1.5	
		prestige = 300
		
		any_pop = { 
			consciousness = -2 
			militancy = -2
			ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = communist }
			ideology = { factor = 0.05 value = socialist } 
		}
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0.1 }
	}
	
}
